function toggleAnoMenu(e){
  e.stopPropagation();
  var menu=document.getElementById('dl-ano-menu');
  if(menu) menu.style.display=menu.style.display==='block'?'none':'block';
}
function toggleDlAno(ano,cb){
  var idx=DL_ANOS_SEL.indexOf(ano);
  if(cb.checked){ if(idx===-1) DL_ANOS_SEL.push(ano); }
  else { if(idx!==-1) DL_ANOS_SEL.splice(idx,1); }
  var lbl=document.getElementById('dl-ano-lbl');
  if(lbl) lbl.textContent=DL_ANOS_SEL.length?DL_ANOS_SEL.slice().sort().join(', '):'Todos';
  renderDesligamentos();
}

function loadDesligamentosData(){
  var kpisEl=document.getElementById('dl-kpis');
  if(kpisEl) kpisEl.innerHTML='<div class="kpi-card" style="grid-column:1/-1"><div class="kpi-label">Carregando dados...</div><div class="spinner" style="margin:8px 0"></div></div>';
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(r){
      if(!r.ok){
        if(kpisEl) kpisEl.innerHTML='<div class="kpi-card" style="grid-column:1/-1;border-color:var(--danger-100)"><div class="kpi-label" style="color:var(--danger-600)">Erro ao carregar desligamentos</div><div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--danger-600)">'+esc(r.error||'Erro desconhecido')+'</div></div>';
        return;
      }
      ALL_DESLIG=r.rows||[];
      initDlFilters();
      renderDesligamentos();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e){
      if(kpisEl) kpisEl.innerHTML='<div class="kpi-card" style="grid-column:1/-1;border-color:var(--danger-100)"><div class="kpi-label" style="color:var(--danger-600)">Erro de comunicação</div><div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--danger-600)">'+esc((e&&e.message)||'Falha na chamada ao servidor')+'</div></div>';
      ALL_DESLIG=[];
    })
    .getDesligamentosData(TOKEN);
}

function initDlFilters(){
  var anos=[...new Set(ALL_DESLIG.map(function(r){ return r.desligAno; }).filter(function(a){ return a>=2023; }))].sort(function(a,b){ return b-a; });
  var unis=[...new Set(ALL_DESLIG.map(function(r){ return r.unidade; }).filter(Boolean))].sort();
  var sets=[...new Set(ALL_DESLIG.map(function(r){ return r.setor; }).filter(Boolean))].sort();
  var aMenu=document.getElementById('dl-ano-menu');
  if(aMenu) aMenu.innerHTML=anos.map(function(a){
    return '<label class="multisel-item"><input type="checkbox" value="'+a+'" onchange="toggleDlAno('+a+',this)"> '+a+'</label>';
  }).join('');
  var uSel=document.getElementById('dl-unidade');
  if(uSel) unis.forEach(function(u){ uSel.appendChild(new Option(u,u)); });
  var sSel=document.getElementById('dl-setor');
  if(sSel) sets.forEach(function(s){ sSel.appendChild(new Option(s,s)); });
}

function getDlFiltered(){
  var fU=v('dl-unidade'),fS=v('dl-setor');
  return ALL_DESLIG.filter(function(r){
    if(!r.desligAno||r.desligAno<2023) return false;
    if(DL_ANOS_SEL.length&&DL_ANOS_SEL.indexOf(r.desligAno)===-1) return false;
    if(fU&&r.unidade!==fU) return false;
    if(fS&&r.setor!==fS) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

function clearDlFilters(){
  DL_ANOS_SEL=[];
  document.querySelectorAll('#dl-ano-menu input[type=checkbox]').forEach(function(cb){ cb.checked=false; });
  var lbl=document.getElementById('dl-ano-lbl'); if(lbl) lbl.textContent='Todos';
  ['dl-unidade','dl-setor'].forEach(function(id){ var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.value=''; });
  renderDesligamentos();
}

function renderDesligamentos(){
  var rows=getDlFiltered();
  renderDlKPIs(rows);
  renderDlTendencia(rows);
  renderDlMotivos(rows);
  renderDlCargo(rows);
  renderDlTempo(rows);
  renderDlSalario(rows);
  renderDlSalCompat(rows);
  renderDlAvaliacoes(rows);
  renderDlInsights(rows);
  renderDlWordCloud(rows);
  renderDlComentarios(rows);
}

function renderDlKPIs(rows){
  var total=rows.length;
  var outra=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.trocaEmpresa&&r.trocaEmpresa!=='Não estou mudando de Empresa'; }).length;
  var pctOutra=total?Math.round(outra/total*100):0;
  var mCounts={};
  rows.forEach(function(r){ (r.motivos||[]).forEach(function(m){ mCounts[m]=(mCounts[m]||0)+1; }); });
  var topMotivo=Object.keys(mCounts).sort(function(a,b){ return mCounts[b]-mCounts[a]; })[0]||'—';
  var posImg=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.eImagem==='Excelente'||r.eImagem==='Bom'; }).length;
  var pctImg=total?Math.round(posImg/total*100):0;
  var fU=v('dl-unidade');
  var demTotal=ALL_EMP.filter(function(e){
    if(e.ativo) return false;
    if(!e.motivoSaida||e.motivoSaida.toLowerCase().indexOf('pedido de demiss')===-1) return false;
    if(!e.desligYear||e.desligYear<2023) return false;
    if(DL_ANOS_SEL.length&&DL_ANOS_SEL.indexOf(e.desligYear)===-1) return false;
    if(fU&&e.unidade!==fU) return false;
    return true;
  }).length;
  var coverage=demTotal?Math.round(total/demTotal*100):null;
  var covColor=coverage===null?'var(--navy-600)':coverage>=80?'var(--success-600)':coverage>=50?'var(--warning-600)':'var(--danger-600)';
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-kpis'); if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML=
    '<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">Total Desligamentos</div><div class="kpi-value">'+total+'</div><div class="kpi-sub">no período selecionado</div></div>'+
    (coverage!==null?'<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">Taxa de Cobertura</div><div class="kpi-value" style="color:'+covColor+'">'+coverage+'%</div><div class="kpi-sub">'+total+' entrevistas · '+demTotal+' pedidos</div></div>':'') +
    '<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">Foram p/ Outra Empresa</div><div class="kpi-value">'+pctOutra+'%</div><div class="kpi-sub">'+outra+' de '+total+' respondentes</div></div>'+
    '<div class="kpi-card highlight"><div class="kpi-label">Principal Motivo</div><div class="kpi-value">'+(mCounts[topMotivo]||0)+'</div><div class="kpi-sub">'+(topMotivo.length>40?esc(topMotivo.slice(0,38))+'…':esc(topMotivo))+' menções</div></div>'+
    '<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">Imagem Positiva BRASAS</div><div class="kpi-value">'+pctImg+'%</div><div class="kpi-sub">avaliaram como Excelente ou Bom</div></div>';
}

function renderDlTendencia(rows){
  var fU=v('dl-unidade');
  var periodKey=function(ano,mes){
    if(DL_PERIODO_VIEW==='anual') return String(ano);
    if(DL_PERIODO_VIEW==='trimestral') return ano+'-Q'+Math.ceil(mes/3);
    return ano+'-'+String(mes).padStart(2,'0');
  };

  // Dataset 1: pedidos de demissão da planilha principal (ALL_EMP), a partir de 2023
  var demGroups={};
  ALL_EMP.forEach(function(e){
    if(e.ativo) return;
    if(!e.motivoSaida||e.motivoSaida.toLowerCase().indexOf('pedido de demiss')===-1) return;
    if(!e.desligYear||!e.desligMonth||e.desligYear<2023) return;
    if(DL_ANOS_SEL.length&&DL_ANOS_SEL.indexOf(e.desligYear)===-1) return;
    if(fU&&e.unidade!==fU) return;
    var k=periodKey(e.desligYear,e.desligMonth);
    demGroups[k]=(demGroups[k]||0)+1;
  });

  // Dataset 2: entrevistas realizadas (ALL_DESLIG já filtrado por getDlFiltered)
  var entGroups={};
  rows.forEach(function(r){
    if(!r.desligAno||!r.desligMes) return;
    var k=periodKey(r.desligAno,r.desligMes);
    entGroups[k]=(entGroups[k]||0)+1;
  });

  var allKeys=[...new Set([...Object.keys(demGroups),...Object.keys(entGroups)])].sort();
  var labels=allKeys.map(function(k){
    if(DL_PERIODO_VIEW==='anual') return k;
    if(DL_PERIODO_VIEW==='trimestral'){ var p=k.split('-Q'); return 'T'+p[1]+'/'+p[0].slice(2); }
    var p=k.split('-'); return MONTHS_PT[parseInt(p[1])-1]+'/'+p[0].slice(2);
  });
  var demVals=allKeys.map(function(k){ return demGroups[k]||0; });
  var entVals=allKeys.map(function(k){ return entGroups[k]||0; });

  var ctx=document.getElementById('chartDlTendencia'); if(!ctx) return;
  if(CHARTS.dlTendencia){ CHARTS.dlTendencia.destroy(); delete CHARTS.dlTendencia; }
  CHARTS.dlTendencia=new Chart(ctx,{
    type:'bar',
    data:{
      labels:labels,
      datasets:[
        {label:'Pedidos de Demissão',data:demVals,backgroundColor:'#2a4d76',borderRadius:4},
        {label:'Entrevistas Realizadas',data:entVals,backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',borderRadius:4}
      ]
    },
    options:{
      responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
      plugins:{
        legend:{display:true,position:'top',labels:{font:{family:'DM Sans',size:12},boxWidth:14,padding:16}},
        tooltip:{callbacks:{label:function(c){ return ' '+c.dataset.label+': '+c.raw; }}}
      },
      scales:{
        y:{beginAtZero:true,ticks:{stepSize:1,font:{family:'DM Sans',size:11}},grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.04)'}},
        x:{ticks:{font:{family:'DM Sans',size:11},maxRotation:DL_PERIODO_VIEW==='mensal'?45:0},grid:{display:false}}
      }
    }
  });
}

function renderDlMotivos(rows){
  var counts={};
  rows.forEach(function(r){ (r.motivos||[]).forEach(function(m){ counts[m]=(counts[m]||0)+1; }); });
  var sorted=Object.keys(counts).sort(function(a,b){ return counts[b]-counts[a]; });
  var maxV=sorted.length?counts[sorted[0]]:1;
  var total=rows.length||1;
  var html=sorted.map(function(m){
    var pct=Math.round(counts[m]/maxV*100);
    var pctTotal=Math.round(counts[m]/total*100);
    return '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:auto 1fr auto;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:5px 0">'+
      '<div style="font-size:.75rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy-700);max-width:240px;min-width:0;white-space:normal;line-height:1.3">'+esc(m)+'</div>'+
      '<div style="background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:20px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:'+pct+'%;height:100%;background:var(--navy-400);border-radius:4px;transition:width .4s"></div></div>'+
      '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--gray-500);white-space:nowrap;min-width:56px;text-align:right"><strong style="color:var(--navy-700)">'+counts[m]+'</strong> ('+pctTotal+'%)</div>'+
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-motivos-bars');
  if(el) el.innerHTML=html||'<div class="table-empty">Sem dados</div>';
}

function renderDlCargo(rows){
  var counts={};
  rows.forEach(function(r){
    var c=r.cargo||'Não informado';
    var cu=c.toUpperCase();
    if(cu.includes('PROFESSOR')) c='Professor';
    else if(cu.includes('SECRETAR')||cu.includes('ASSISTENTE ADM')) c='Secretaria / Adm';
    else if(cu.includes('MARKETING')||cu.includes('MIDIA')) c='Marketing';
    else if(cu.includes('ESTAGIÁR')||cu.includes('ESTAGIARIO')) c='Estagiário';
    else if(cu.includes('ASG')||cu.includes('PORTEIRO')||cu.includes('PINTOR')) c='Serviços Gerais';
    else if(cu.includes('GERENTE')||cu.includes('COORDENADOR')||cu.includes('DIRETOR')) c='Gestão';
    else if(cu.includes('ANALISTA')||cu.includes('ASSISTENTE')) c='Analista / Assistente';
    counts[c]=(counts[c]||0)+1;
  });
  var sorted=Object.keys(counts).sort(function(a,b){ return counts[b]-counts[a]; });
  var maxV=sorted.length?counts[sorted[0]]:1;
  var total=rows.length||1;
  var colors=['#2a4d76','#3d6b99','#5a8aba','#0d9488','#22c55e','#f59e0b','#8b5cf6','#ef4444'];
  var html=sorted.map(function(c,i){
    var pct=Math.round(counts[c]/maxV*100);
    var pctTotal=Math.round(counts[c]/total*100);
    return '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:160px 1fr auto;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:5px 0">'+
      '<div style="font-size:.8rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy-700)">'+esc(c)+'</div>'+
      '<div style="background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:22px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:'+pct+'%;height:100%;background:'+colors[i%colors.length]+';border-radius:4px;transition:width .4s"></div></div>'+
      '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--gray-500);min-width:60px;text-align:right"><strong style="color:var(--navy-700)">'+counts[c]+'</strong> ('+pctTotal+'%)</div>'+
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-cargo-bars');
  if(el) el.innerHTML=html||'<div class="table-empty">Sem dados</div>';
}

function renderDlTempo(rows){
  var counts={};
  DL_TEMPO_ORDER.forEach(function(t){ counts[t]=0; });
  rows.forEach(function(r){ if(r.tempoEmpresa&&counts[r.tempoEmpresa]!==undefined) counts[r.tempoEmpresa]++; });
  var maxV=Math.max.apply(null,DL_TEMPO_ORDER.map(function(t){ return counts[t]; }).concat([1]));
  var total=rows.length||1;
  var html=DL_TEMPO_ORDER.map(function(t){
    var n=counts[t]; if(!n) return '';
    var pct=Math.round(n/maxV*100);
    var pctTotal=Math.round(n/total*100);
    return '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:130px 1fr auto;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:5px 0">'+
      '<div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy-700)">'+t+'</div>'+
      '<div style="background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:20px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:'+pct+'%;height:100%;background:var(--teal-600);border-radius:4px;transition:width .4s"></div></div>'+
      '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--gray-500);min-width:56px;text-align:right"><strong style="color:var(--navy-700)">'+n+'</strong> ('+pctTotal+'%)</div>'+
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-tempo-bars');
  if(el) el.innerHTML=html||'<div class="table-empty">Sem dados</div>';
}

function renderDlSalario(rows){
  var faixas=['Até 10%','11% a 30%','31% a 50%','Mais de 50%','Mais de 100%'];
  var counts={}; faixas.forEach(function(f){ counts[f]=0; });
  rows.forEach(function(r){
    if(r.trocaEmpresa&&r.trocaEmpresa!=='Não estou mudando de Empresa'&&counts[r.trocaEmpresa]!==undefined)
      counts[r.trocaEmpresa]++;
  });
  var ctx=document.getElementById('chartDlSalario'); if(!ctx) return;
  if(CHARTS.dlSalario){ CHARTS.dlSalario.destroy(); delete CHARTS.dlSalario; }
  CHARTS.dlSalario=new Chart(ctx,{
    type:'bar',
    data:{labels:faixas,datasets:[{data:faixas.map(function(f){ return counts[f]; }),backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',borderRadius:4}]},
    options:{
      responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
      plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:function(ctx){ return ' '+ctx.raw+' pessoas'; }}}},
      scales:{
        y:{beginAtZero:true,ticks:{stepSize:1,font:{family:'DM Sans',size:11}},grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.04)'}},
        x:{ticks:{font:{family:'DM Sans',size:11}},grid:{display:false}}
      }
    }
  });
}

function renderDlSalCompat(rows){
  var sim=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.salCompat==='Sim'; }).length;
  var nao=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.salCompat==='Não'||r.salCompat==='Nao'; }).length;
  var total=sim+nao||1;
  var pSim=Math.round(sim/total*100), pNao=Math.round(nao/total*100);
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-sal-compat'); if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML=
    '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:12px">'+
      '<span style="min-width:38px;font-size:.82rem;color:var(--navy-700);font-weight:600">Sim</span>'+
      '<div style="flex:1;background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:26px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:'+pSim+'%;height:100%;background:var(--success-500);transition:width .4s"></div></div>'+
      '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--navy-700);min-width:70px;text-align:right">'+sim+' ('+pSim+'%)</span>'+
    '</div>'+
    '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:20px">'+
      '<span style="min-width:38px;font-size:.82rem;color:var(--navy-700);font-weight:600">Não</span>'+
      '<div style="flex:1;background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:26px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:'+pNao+'%;height:100%;background:var(--danger-500);transition:width .4s"></div></div>'+
      '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.8rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--navy-700);min-width:70px;text-align:right">'+nao+' ('+pNao+'%)</span>'+
    '</div>'+
    '<div style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--gray-400);text-align:center">'+(sim+nao)+' respondentes</div>';
}

function renderDlAvaliacoes(rows){
  var ratings=['Excelente','Bom','Regular','Ruim'];
  var scoreMap={Excelente:4,Bom:3,Regular:2,Ruim:1};

  // Cards de nota média por categoria — identifica a de menor nota
  var catAvgs=DL_AVAL_GROUPS.map(function(group){
    var sum=0,count=0;
    group.items.forEach(function(item){
      rows.forEach(function(r){
        var s=scoreMap[r[item.field]];
        if(s!==undefined){ sum+=s; count++; }
      });
    });
    return {title:group.title,avg:count?sum/count:null};
  });
  var worstIdx=-1, worstAvg=Infinity;
  catAvgs.forEach(function(c,i){ if(c.avg!==null&&c.avg<worstAvg){ worstAvg=c.avg; worstIdx=i; } });
  var kpisHtml=catAvgs.map(function(c,i){
    var avg=c.avg;
    var isWorst=(i===worstIdx&&avg!==null);
    var color=avg===null?'var(--gray-400)':avg>=3.5?'var(--success-600)':avg>=2.5?'var(--navy-600)':avg>=1.5?'var(--warning-600)':'var(--danger-600)';
    var bg=avg===null?'':avg>=3.5?'background:var(--success-50)':avg>=2.5?'background:var(--navy-50)':avg>=1.5?'background:var(--warning-50)':'background:var(--danger-50)';
    var border=isWorst?';border-bottom:3px solid var(--warning-500)':'';
    var badge=isWorst?'<span style="display:inline-block;font-size:.65rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--warning-600);background:var(--warning-100);border-radius:4px;padding:1px 6px;margin-top:4px">⚠ ponto crítico</span>':'';
    return '<div class="kpi-card" style="'+bg+border+'">'+
      '<div class="kpi-label">'+esc(c.title)+'</div>'+
      '<div class="kpi-value" style="color:'+color+'">'+(avg!==null?avg.toFixed(1):'—')+'</div>'+
      '<div class="kpi-sub">nota de 1 a 4</div>'+
      badge+
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
  var kpisEl=document.getElementById('dl-aval-kpis');
  if(kpisEl) kpisEl.innerHTML=kpisHtml;

  // Barras empilhadas detalhadas por item
  var legend=ratings.map(function(r){
    return '<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;margin-right:14px;font-size:.75rem">'+
      '<span style="display:inline-block;width:12px;height:12px;border-radius:2px;background:'+DL_AVAL_COLORS[r]+'"></span>'+r+'</span>';
  }).join('');
  var html=DL_AVAL_GROUPS.map(function(group){
    var items=group.items.map(function(item){
      var c={'Excelente':0,'Bom':0,'Regular':0,'Ruim':0},tot=0;
      rows.forEach(function(r){
        var val=r[item.field];
        if(val&&val!=='Não Optante'&&val!=='Nao Optante'&&c[val]!==undefined){ c[val]++; tot++; }
      });
      if(!tot) return '<div class="dl-aval-row"><span class="dl-aval-label">'+esc(item.label)+'</span><div class="dl-aval-bar-wrap"></div><span class="dl-aval-score" style="color:var(--gray-300)">—</span></div>';
      var segs=ratings.map(function(r){
        var p=Math.round(c[r]/tot*100); if(!p) return '';
        return '<div title="'+r+': '+p+'% ('+c[r]+')" style="height:100%;width:'+p+'%;background:'+DL_AVAL_COLORS[r]+';flex-shrink:0"></div>';
      }).join('');
      var score=(c['Excelente']*4+c['Bom']*3+c['Regular']*2+c['Ruim']*1)/tot;
      var sColor=score>=3.5?'var(--success-600)':score>=2.5?'var(--navy-600)':score>=1.5?'var(--warning-600)':'var(--danger-600)';
      return '<div class="dl-aval-row"><span class="dl-aval-label">'+esc(item.label)+'</span><div class="dl-aval-bar-wrap">'+segs+'</div><span class="dl-aval-score" style="color:'+sColor+'">'+score.toFixed(1)+'</span></div>';
    }).join('');
    return '<div class="dl-aval-group"><div class="dl-aval-group-title">'+esc(group.title)+'</div>'+items+'</div>';
  }).join('');
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-avaliacoes');
  if(el) el.innerHTML='<div style="margin-bottom:16px">'+legend+'</div>'+html;
}

function renderDlInsights(rows){
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-insights'); if(!el) return;

  var withC=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.comentario&&r.comentario.length>8; });
  if(!withC.length){ el.innerHTML='<div class="table-empty">Nenhum comentário para analisar</div>'; return; }

  var normalize=function(s){ return s.toLowerCase().normalize('NFD').replace(/[̀-ͯ]/g,''); };
  var themeCounts=DL_COMMENT_THEMES.map(function(t){
    var cnt=withC.filter(function(r){
      var text=normalize(r.comentario);
      return t.keys.some(function(k){ return text.indexOf(normalize(k))!==-1; });
    }).length;
    return {label:t.label,count:cnt};
  }).filter(function(t){ return t.count>0; }).sort(function(a,b){ return b.count-a.count; });

  if(!themeCounts.length){ el.innerHTML='<div class="table-empty">Nenhum tema identificado</div>'; return; }

  var maxT=themeCounts[0].count;
  var barColors=['#2a4d76','#3d6b99','#0d9488','#8b5cf6','#f97316','#22c55e','#ec4899'];
  el.innerHTML=
    '<div style="font-size:.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--gray-500);letter-spacing:.06em;margin-bottom:14px">TEMAS MENCIONADOS NOS COMENTÁRIOS <span style="font-weight:400">('+withC.length+' comentário'+(withC.length!==1?'s':'')+')</span></div>'+
    themeCounts.map(function(t,i){
      var pct=Math.round(t.count/maxT*100);
      var pctCom=Math.round(t.count/withC.length*100);
      return '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:180px 1fr 80px;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:4px 0">'+
        '<div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--navy-700);font-weight:500">'+esc(t.label)+'</div>'+
        '<div style="background:var(--gray-100);border-radius:4px;height:18px;overflow:hidden">'+
          '<div style="width:'+pct+'%;height:100%;background:'+barColors[i%barColors.length]+';border-radius:4px;transition:width .4s"></div>'+
        '</div>'+
        '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--gray-500);text-align:right"><strong style="color:var(--navy-700)">'+t.count+'</strong> ('+pctCom+'%)</div>'+
      '</div>';
    }).join('');
}

    var text=(r.comentario||'')+' '+(r.motivoOutros||'');
    allSeqs.push(
      text.split(/[\s,;:.!?()[\]{}"'\/\\|]+/)
        .map(function(w){ return norm(w.replace(/[^a-zà-ÿ]/gi,'')); })
    );
  });

  // Conta palavras individuais significativas (mín. 4 letras)
  var counts={};
  allSeqs.forEach(function(tokens){
    tokens.forEach(function(w){
      if(w.length<4||STOPS.has(w)) return;
      counts[w]=(counts[w]||0)+1;
    });
  });

  // Extrai bigramas: dois tokens significativos consecutivos
  var bigramCounts={};
  allSeqs.forEach(function(tokens){
    var sig=tokens.map(function(w){ return (w.length>=4&&!STOPS.has(w))?w:null; });
    for(var i=0;i<tokens.length-1;i++){
      if(sig[i]&&sig[i+1]) bigramCounts[sig[i]+' '+sig[i+1]]=(bigramCounts[sig[i]+' '+sig[i+1]]||0)+1;
    }
  });

  var sortedWords=Object.entries(counts).filter(function(e){ return e[1]>=2; }).sort(function(a,b){ return b[1]-a[1]; }).slice(0,35);
  var sortedBigrams=Object.entries(bigramCounts).filter(function(e){ return e[1]>=2; }).sort(function(a,b){ return b[1]-a[1]; }).slice(0,18);

  var combined=sortedBigrams.map(function(e){ return {w:e[0],f:e[1],bigram:true}; })
    .concat(sortedWords.map(function(e){ return {w:e[0],f:e[1],bigram:false}; }));

  if(!combined.length){ el.innerHTML='<div class="table-empty">Palavras insuficientes (nenhuma com 2+ menções)</div>'; if(badge) badge.textContent='0'; return; }

  var allF=combined.map(function(c){ return c.f; });
  var maxF=Math.max.apply(null,allF), minF=Math.min.apply(null,allF), range=maxF-minF||1;

  var top=combined.slice(0,10), rest=combined.slice(10);
  for(var i=rest.length-1;i>0;i--){ var j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(i+1)); var t=rest[i]; rest[i]=rest[j]; rest[j]=t; }
  combined=top.concat(rest);

  if(badge) badge.textContent=(sortedBigrams.length?sortedBigrams.length+' frases · ':'')+sortedWords.length+' palavras';

  el.innerHTML=combined.map(function(item){
    var word=item.w, freq=item.f, isBigram=item.bigram;
    var scale=(freq-minF)/range;
    var size=(0.78+scale*1.45).toFixed(2);
    var weight=scale>0.6?'700':scale>0.3?'600':'400';
    var words=item.w.split(' ');
    var hasPOS=words.some(function(w){ return POSITIVE.has(w); });
    var hasNEG=words.some(function(w){ return NEGATIVE.has(w); });
    var color,bg;
    if(hasPOS&&!hasNEG){ color='var(--success-600)'; bg='var(--success-50)'; }
    else if(hasNEG&&!hasPOS){ color='var(--danger-600)'; bg='var(--danger-50)'; }
    else { color='var(--navy-600)'; bg='var(--navy-50)'; }
    var extra=isBigram?';border:1.5px dashed currentColor':'';
    return '<span class="wc-word" title="'+freq+' menção'+(freq!==1?'ões':'')+'" style="font-size:'+size+'rem;font-weight:'+weight+';color:'+color+';background:'+bg+extra+'">'+esc(word)+'</span>';
  }).join('');
}

function renderDlComentarios(rows){
  var withC=rows.filter(function(r){ return r.comentario&&r.comentario.length>10; });
  var countEl=document.getElementById('dl-comments-count');
  if(countEl) countEl.textContent=withC.length;
  var el=document.getElementById('dl-comments-list'); if(!el) return;
  if(!withC.length){ el.innerHTML='<div class="table-empty">Nenhum comentário no período</div>'; return; }
  el.innerHTML=withC.slice().reverse().slice(0,25).map(function(r){
    return '<div class="dl-comment-card">'+
      '<div class="dl-comment-meta">'+
        '<strong style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--navy-800)">'+esc(r.nome)+'</strong>'+
        (r.cargo?'<span class="dl-comment-badge">'+esc(r.cargo)+'</span>':'')+
        (r.unidade?'<span class="dl-comment-badge">'+esc(r.unidade)+'</span>':'')+
        '<span style="margin-left:auto;font-size:.72rem;color:var(--gray-400)">'+esc(r.dataDeslig)+'</span>'+
      '</div>'+
      '<p class="dl-comment-text">'+esc(r.comentario)+'</p>'+
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

// UTILS
function v(id,def){ def=def||''; var el=document.getElementById(id); return el?(el.value||def):def; }
function set(id,val){ var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.textContent=val; }
function fmt(n){ return(n===null||n===undefined)?'—':Number(n).toLocaleString('pt-BR'); }
function pct(a,b){ return b?Math.round(a/b*100):0; }
function avg(arr){ return arr.length?arr.reduce(function(s,n){ return s+n; },0)/arr.length:0; }
function esc(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
function validNum(x){ return x!==null&&x!==undefined&&!isNaN(x)&&isFinite(x); }
function fmtNow(){ var n=new Date(); return n.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR')+' às '+n.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'}); }
function groupBy(arr,key){ return arr.reduce(function(acc,e){ var k=e[key]||'(não informado)'; if(!acc[k]) acc[k]=[]; acc[k].push(e); return acc; },{}); }
function toISO(str){ if(!str||str==='—') return ''; var m=str.match(/^(\d{2})\/(\d{2})\/(\d{4})$/); return m?m[3]+'-'+m[2]+'-'+m[1]:''; }
function fmtDateBr(val){
  if(!val) return '—';
  var d=new Date(val);
  if(isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(val);
  return String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')+'/'+String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'/'+d.getFullYear();
}
</script>
